          <input id="search" type="search" autocomplete="off" name="q" value="" class="input-text required-entry" maxlength="128" placeholder="Enter Keywords">

           <li> <input type="radio" name="search-filter" checked id="productSelection" value="product"><label for="productSelection">Products</label> </li> 
           <li> <input type="radio" name="search-filter" id="supportSelection" value="support"><label for="supportSelection">Support</label> </li> 
          </ul>

         <script type="text/javascript">
     function searchTopForm(obj) {
         var form = $j(obj);
         var value = form.find('input#search').val();
         if (value!='') {
             var filter = form.find('input[name=search-filter]:checked').val();
             if (filter=='support') {
                  form.attr('action', 'https://misfit.com/catalogsearch/result/support/');
             } else {
                  form.attr('action', 'https://misfit.com/catalogsearch/result/');
             }
             return true;
         }
         return false;
     }
  </script> 
        </form> </li>

     function searchTopForm(obj) {
         var form = $j(obj);
         var value = form.find('input#search').val();
         if (value!='') {
             var filter = form.find('input[name=search-filter]:checked').val();
             if (filter=='support') {
                  form.attr('action', 'https://misfit.com/catalogsearch/result/support/');
             } else {
                  form.attr('action', 'https://misfit.com/catalogsearch/result/');
             }
             return true;
         }
         return false;
     }

            <div class="text-block"> 
             <h2>Smart Accessories That Have High Style IQ</h2> 
             <p>Misfit isnt just in the business of activity trackers and sleep monitors, but technology is where we found our inspiring startand we havent rested yet. We keep pushing smart technology forward with smart accessories, exclusives, and gear that integrates with our products making your life better and a whole lot smarter.</p> 
             <div id="show-hide" class="content-show-hide" style="display: none;"> 
              <p>Everyone has their own style, and now more than ever they have options when it comes to wearing their smart accessory. A sport band is a must for sweating it out at the gym, and with our three-color sport band pack, you can change the color based on how you feel that day. And while those sport bands may be totally enviableand a mustin the gym, they may look slightly out of place with a cocktail dress. Thats why we have more than just sporty interchangeable straps for our devices. From a handsome pebbled leather strap ora striking metal mesh band to accessories for our Swarovski Activity Crystal and Ekocycle Shine collections, there is something for men and women looking for more of a unique look to their smart accessories. Wish there was another way to wear your Misfit smart device? Weve got pendants that range from sleek and modern to vintage-inspired and even eye-catching bling.</p> 
              <h2>Go Undercover In Smart Gear</h2> 
              <p>Youre probably already pretty busy these days, so when youre picking out the latest smart accessories for your device, consider that we also offer some gear that goes undercover with inner pockets to hold your Misfit device. But its stuff you already needed anyway, so we think of it as a win-win. Youd never know by looking at them, but our classic or high-performance tech tees and sport socks have small inner pockets, which all conveniently fit your device. Pretty smart, huh?</p> 
              <h2>Get The Latest on Misfit Exclusives</h2> 
              <p>Because were committed to innovation, there will be lots of Misfit exclusives in the future. Like ultra-premium box sets exquisitely crafted from pure Sapele Mahogany wood. Each box contains your choice of a Champagne or Coral Misfit Shine, Bloom Necklace, rubber sport band, magnetic clasp, battery, tool and instruction guide.We like to think of smart technology in the most innovative ways. If we surprise you or even introduce you to something that inspires you, weve done our job. </p> 
              <p>In November Misfit partnered with BaubleBar to introduce the Helena Necklace and Helena Bracelet featuring vintage accents with classic BaubleBar sparkle. The secret is in the locket on the necklace or bracelet, which opens to reveal our Flash fitness tracker. These fashion-forward smart accessories are as smart as they are stunning.</p> 
              <h2>Shining A Light On Smart Light Bulbs</h2> 
              <p>By now, you may have gotten the idea that were into helping you improve your life by helping you understand how your daily and fitness activities add up. We also strive to improve your quality of life. We think if you start the day off the rightwith enough quality sleepeverything has a better chance of falling into place. We all react to light differently, especially when it interrupts a nice dream.</p> 
              <p>Misfit Bolt is a wireless, connected light bulb with smart technology that lets you personalize your home lighting to create the space you wantmorning to nightand produces light equal to a typical 60-watt bulb. It connects with Misfit Shine and Flash and can perform functions synchronized with our fitness trackers. This includes waking up with a custom light that turns on and is in line with the sleep pattern suggested by the activity tracker.</p> 
              <p>You dont have to be a prodigy. We promise, there are no complicated hubs or setup needed. Transform your home easily through your mobile phone using our Misfit Home mobile app. Easy as that.</p>
